These components include:\n\nOne block finality: This feature ensures that transactions are confirmed and finalized with each block, providing a high level of security and efficiency.\n\nOracle: Neo incorporates an oracle system that allows external data to be securely integrated into smart contracts, expanding the platform's capabilities.\n\nNeoFS: NeoFS is a decentralized storage network within the Neo blockchain. Its key components include digital assets, digital identity, and smart contracts. With its upgraded version, Neo N3, and core technologies such as dBFT, NeoVM, NeoX, and NeoFS, the platform provides enhanced scalability, security, and interoperability.
